API -->Application Programming Interface

webservices -->HTTP 

UI -->UserInterface testing -->front end 
API->Backend testing

API testing:
Documentation-->Swagger
Endpoint -->uri /resource
RequestMethod -->create,read, update and delete  (POST,GET,PATCH/PUT,DELETE)
Headers -->tokens(Authentication) -->requesttype /response type
Body/Payload -->(Testdata)-->fristname
{

}

Response -response status code/time/text 200,201,400,404,403,500

Parameters-path and query parater

path -->specific resource

Http Methods -->verbs/CRUD operation
Post -->to create a resource
Get -->to fetch the resource
Delete-->to delete the specific resource
Patch -->partial update in the resource
Put -->replace the resource info , if not available creates a new resource

Authentication->Who are you vs Authorization-->what can you alowed to do
what permission you have given to access the application

no auth -->weather api 
Basic auth -->username, password
OAuth -->token
apikey -->token 
JWT -->json webtoken

Salesforce

-->endpoint
-->OAuth
-->RequestMethod
-->Requestbody
-->responsebody/stauscode/status text

Response

201 created -->post
200 ok -->get
204 No content -->pathch & delete

415 unsupported media type-->any headers are wrong  
404 Not found -->resource doesnot exist
400 BadRequest -->payload/body info is wrong
401 Unauthorized -->session expired
